  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_66d0afcb-07e5-4e7c-9187-4e0ae879fabb'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_552').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>

<div id="review_379628602" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/379628602" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/379628602?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer379628602" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3204782091452408399">4.5 stars!<br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385743i/744819.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> A rock-star romance with a paranormal twist!<br/><br/>I totally loved this book!! It grabbed a hold of me and I didn't want to put it down for a second! </b><br/><br/>The sexual tension, the banter, the twists, the one-liners, the characters - everything about this book was awesome!<br/><br/>Reeling from the death of her brother, Grace goes home to her best friend who drags her out to a bar where she meets Shane - a deliciously gorgeous, tattooed, rock god guitarist/singer who, despite his man-whoring reputation, she </span>
  <span id="freeText3204782091452408399" style="display:none">4.5 stars!<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385743i/744819.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> A rock-star romance with a paranormal twist!<br><br>I totally loved this book!! It grabbed a hold of me and I didn't want to put it down for a second! </b><br><br>The sexual tension, the banter, the twists, the one-liners, the characters - everything about this book was awesome!<br><br>Reeling from the death of her brother, Grace goes home to her best friend who drags her out to a bar where she meets Shane - a deliciously gorgeous, tattooed, rock god guitarist/singer who, despite his man-whoring reputation, she can't help but feel intensely drawn too.<br><br>But Grace has a secret. One that now only her best friend knows and despite how much she feels drawn to Shane, she's has to hold back because she is searching, and has been searching for the whole of her existence, for the love of her life. Her angel she was once torn away from.<br><br>I went into this book blind. I took a trusted friend's advice who told me to just read it and not try and find out any of the twists or tidbits in advance and I am so glad!!! (lol, so my review is spoiler-free)<br><br>Shane was pretty much the perfect recipe for yumminess and, just like Grace, I couldn't help but be drawn to him. Despite how he seemed on the surface, there was so much depth to his character which came out in little bits an pieces as the book went on. I fell reeeally hard for him. He was like a delicious blend of Travis and Kellan mixed in with a bit of a tortured soul. Pure yumminess &lt;3<br><br><i> <b> "...I want you to tell me what I need to do to be a good enough man for you." </b> </i> *swoooon*<br><br>I did really love that despite swooning pretty heavily over Shane, Grace had no desire to be another notch in his bed post and held her ground waiting for what she felt was right.<br><br><i> "...do yourself a favor, don't bother trying to mess with my head, it'll be a waste of your time. I won't sleep with you. Just treat me like one of the guys and we'll get along just fine..."<br>He blinked and hesitated... Then a devilish smile crept across his face, "Who said I wanted to sleep with you? You're just one of the guys, I don't do guys...Although, I have to admit. You are the sexiest guy I've ever met." </i><br><br>But because of this situation, the sexual tension between them is INTENSE!! It sizzled. You felt it. My heart was racing. I couldn't stop reading!! And the banter was brilliant - the digs, the ribs, the teasing...<br><br><i> "Please, save your breath, because you might need it to blow up your date later." </i><br><br>I loved how subtly the paranormal aspect of this book built. For the first half of the book just reads like a regular contemporary romance but while dropping little hints and clues along the way leaving you wondering and guessing and then when it hits and the twist is revealed, I swear it gave me chills. I loved the concept!<br><br>And it wasn't just the twist that built up - there was so much more to the story that even on its own was thrilling - the music, the intensity of the chemistry between Shane and Grace, that undeniable pull... add that to a wonderful group of side characters and you have yourself a really fun read.<br><br>The music aspect of this book was phenomenal - the scenes where they played, both on and off stage, gave me shivers. Both Grace and Shane play guitar and sing and seeing them in their music element just magnified the UST between them to pretty epic proportions!<br><br>I'll admit, I did go through some some moments of frustration with the heroine but they weren't enough to detract from the story.<br><br>There is sort of a hint of a love triangle at the beginning of the story - but don't worry, it doesn't go anywhere :)<br><br>And okay, so it wasn't the most phenomenally edited book ever written - yes there was an inconsistency or two and yes there were a few noticeable errors, but who cares?!? Personally, if the story is strong enough, I'm totally happy to overlook those errors. So yes, they were there, but I easily overlooked them and kept reading. I'll just say though that with a proper edit, this book could easily end up on my fav's shelf!<br><br>The book has kind of got a little bit of a Beautiful Disaster/Thoughtless feel to it with a paranormal twist. Its not quite the same as them but you'll definitely see the similarities if you read it. <br><br>While this book has no sex in it but I didn't miss it even for a second. I wouldn't call this book 'tame'. The sexual tension is so steamy that that alone had me fanning myself!! and I hear that book 2 takes the steam to the next level so... SQUEE!!<br><br><i> <b> "Please, Grace, whatever it is you're going after, please try and find it here with me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be." </b></i> <br><br>The ending was intense and with a cliffhanger like that, I am soooooooo freaking glad the second book is out now!! *runs off to go get it*<br><br>**Both this book and the sequel are only $1.50 on Amazon right now so for those prices, you can't really go wrong! :)<br><br>CASTING: <br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380385743i/744820._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3204782091452408399" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1007653339198528554"><b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849639.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Well I hope so!<br/><br/>*keeping fingers crossed*<br/><br/><br/>This is a story of two soulmates trying to find each other...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849640.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I have to say that I'm really surprised I enjoyed this book so much, and I am uber-excited about the other two books, especially Shane's POV! OMG I can't wait!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>The story</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849641.gif' alt='Image Hosted by ImageShack.us' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>In this book we get Grace's POV, and slowly learn about her past, who she is, and who she's looking for.<br/><br/>After the death of her brother, Grace goes to her best friend Lea, the only person in the world who knows her secret.<br/>There sh</span>
  <span id="freeText1007653339198528554" style="display:none"><b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849639.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Well I hope so!<br><br>*keeping fingers crossed*<br><br><br>This is a story of two soulmates trying to find each other...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849640.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><br>I have to say that I'm really surprised I enjoyed this book so much, and I am uber-excited about the other two books, especially Shane's POV! OMG I can't wait!!!<br><br><br><br><br>The story</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849641.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>In this book we get Grace's POV, and slowly learn about her past, who she is, and who she's looking for.<br><br>After the death of her brother, Grace goes to her best friend Lea, the only person in the world who knows her secret.<br>There she meets Shane, the lead singer of the Mad World band, a guy that is pure perfection, except for his one night stands and millions of grupies wanting to have sex with him.<br>But that doesn't matter anyway because all Grace wants is to find her soul mate, the one she's been looking for for centuries.<br><br><br><br><br><b>The writing</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849642.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This book had so much errors it isn't even funny. It could do with a good editor. A really really really good editor.<br>I'm half illiterate and I noticed them, so I'm guessing there are even more that I didn't notice :D<br>Anyway, it could use some polishing and I'd love to see that happen cause it really has potential to be a fantastic book after it's done :DD<br>The story and dialogue were interesting and it made me love the book even with the less than stellar writing, so that's saying something :D<br><br><br><br><br><b>Grace</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849643.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>First of all, you have to know that Grace has an awesome personality!<br>She is so funny and I just loved reading about her, which is a plus since this book is in her POV.<br>Her dates with Tucker were hilarious and the sushi bar scene is my favorite :DDDD<br><br>BUT!<br><br>As for her intellect, she is pretty much stupid as hell.<br>Seriously, for someone who has lived for centuries, she is uber-dumb.<br>I mean, she's looking for her "The One" guy, and is willing to give a chance to a slimeball like Tucker, who makes her sick to her stomach, and refuses to even contemplate the possibility that it could be someone who attracts her like crazy, someone who she can't stop thinking about, someone who she wants and someone who wants her back.<br>No that would be stupid and wouldn't make any sense at all, right????????<br>*sigh*<br>That's the one thing that bothered me here, she took everyone into the equation for her possible soulmate, except one guy.<br><br><br><br><br><b>Shane</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849644.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>He is amazing :)<br>Although I am not a fan of rock stars and such in books, I loved Shane here!! &lt;3<br>From the first time he sees Grace, he wants to be with her, but of course, she refuses him all the time :(<br>So poor Shane tries to be her friend of he can't get anything more from her.<br>He is just uber-sweet and swoony most of the time, and protective and jealous the rest of it :D<br>I am just dying to read his POV, OMG!! &lt;3<br><br><br><br><br><b>Overall<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380425651ra/849645.gif" alt="Image Hosted by ImageShack.us" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Even though this could've been written a bit better, and it could've had a bit more intelligent heroine, I still enjoyed it, hell, I loved it!<br>So all I can say is, if you're looking for brilliant writing, you may not find it here, but the story is fun and exciting, and the romance wonderful and swoony &lt;3 I know I am definitely looking forward to the other two books!!<br><br>Oh and beware, this one has a cliffie so have the second book close to you if you decide to read it ;)<br><br></b><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="1007653339198528554" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_429517713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/429517713" />
    <a title="Ailyne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12102232-ailyne"><img alt="Ailyne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1588439987p2/12102232.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/429517713?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ailyne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ailyne" href="/user/show/12102232-ailyne">Ailyne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer429517713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9678324737410263284">Alrigh! Alright! Alright!...That had to be the most erotic book I have read in a while...<b>AND IT DOESNT EVEN HAVE SEX IN IT!</b><br/><a href='http://www.sodahead.com/fun/thank-god-its-friday-party/question-2869291/?link=ibaf&imgurl=http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bTd84paIfzk/TZQchtI-RaI/AAAAAAAAARs/ycMTzDa2brE/s1600/santana%252520fanning%252520herself.gif&q=fanning%20yourself+gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/428090.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  <br/>
</a><br/>Lets start off with the one character that has caused all women to lose their ovaries. Shane. <b>SHANE-FREAKING-PERFECT-GOD-WHO-I-WANT-TO-DIP-IN-CHOCOLATE-AND-DEVOUR!</b> Too bad I will never be able to bare children...my ovaries are no longer in existence...and I'm willing to bet my fallopian tubes went right along with them. <br/><br/><a href='http://media.photobucket.com/image/ovaries%20gif/blackonice/GIFS/gif_ovariestonystark.gif?o=4' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/613343.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>So this book is about this girl named Grace </span>
  <span id="freeText9678324737410263284" style="display:none">Alrigh! Alright! Alright!...That had to be the most erotic book I have read in a while...<b>AND IT DOESNT EVEN HAVE SEX IN IT!</b><br><a href="http://www.sodahead.com/fun/thank-god-its-friday-party/question-2869291/?link=ibaf&amp;imgurl=http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-bTd84paIfzk/TZQchtI-RaI/AAAAAAAAARs/ycMTzDa2brE/s1600/santana%252520fanning%252520herself.gif&amp;q=fanning%20yourself+gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/428090.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
</a><br>Lets start off with the one character that has caused all women to lose their ovaries. Shane. <b>SHANE-FREAKING-PERFECT-GOD-WHO-I-WANT-TO-DIP-IN-CHOCOLATE-AND-DEVOUR!</b> Too bad I will never be able to bare children...my ovaries are no longer in existence...and I'm willing to bet my fallopian tubes went right along with them. <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/ovaries%20gif/blackonice/GIFS/gif_ovariestonystark.gif?o=4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/613343.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So this book is about this girl named Grace who is destined to walk the Earth for all eternity looking for the angel she fell in love with eons ago. Shane is an egotistical and gorgeous guy who sings for a band called Mad World. Grace and Shane meet, have a couple of steamy moments and then some really creepy things start to happen.<br><br>This book's appeal depends heavily on the mystery aspect so I can't really throw out too many details without ruining the book or confusing the hell out of you, but I will tell you my feelings on the story. As I said before Shane practically had me on the verge of a bookgasm. He just oozes sex and even through the author does a frustratingly beautiful job of describing just how sexy he is, we never get to plunge into those waters as deeply as we start to hope. Grace pissed me off in the beginning with her whining and feeling sorry for herself, but she gradually grows a a pair and toughens up...so I ended up liking her. I like her witty personality and her attitude towards her "borrowed" body. Together Shane and Grace are one ticking time bomb I personally wanted the pleasure of detonating...unfortunately as soon as the clock read 0:01 the ninja bomb disarmers came in..more than once. So much sexual tension builds up between Shane and Grace it's ridiculous...sigh <br><br>This is what kept happening...!! :P<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393584ra/757781.gif" width="400" height="300/" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also really liked Grace's best friend, she knows the truth about Grace and the love of her life, she is also really funny and a support channel for Grace. Gabriel creeped me the freak out...from the beginning I was like eww...he sounds hot and everything but I didn't like him from the moment he came in...Shane's band members and friends are pretty adorable except for Tucker...I wanted to punch him...he needed to get punched. <br><br>Before all of you jump through my computer and mug me for only giving this book three stars, hear me out...or in this case..read me out haha. As soon as I started Fall From Grace I begin to notice that the style of writing was very simple...overly simple in fact. I felt like I was reading a fourth grade narrative essay ( and I teach 4th grade reading so I would know) which threw me off a bit until I got enveloped in the actual story. Writing style is very important for me when it comes to creating a picture in my head, so that is where the two stars were deducted from; however, the concept, story, characters, and love scenes blew my mind all the way to Pluto (who is regrettably no longer considered a planet).<br> <br>Of course ...the much dreaded cliffhanger left me wanting to kick something...and i did...my poor pillowpet is going to report me to the domestic abuse hotline. oh well...off I go to read the next book...maybe I'll get my ovaries back or maybe ill end up losing my bladder too. </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/433625698" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/433625698?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Duchess Nicole by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/3769295-dawn">Dawn</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=recommendations">recommendations</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=z-no-bueno">z-no-bueno</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=buddy-reads">buddy-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-new-adult">genre-new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-paranormal-other">genre-paranormal-other</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer433625698" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10411705230141911193"><b>2.5 Stars (that last half star is for the parts in between 60-90%)<br/>Don't hate me!!!!!!!</b><br/><br/>Miss for me, for the most part. I almost stopped reading this one, in fact. My rule of thumb for dnf is that I must wait until I hit the 65% mark. If I still can't stand it enough by then and I'm able to skip the last 35% of the book, then it <i>really</i> isn't holding my interest. And I still feel justified rating and reviewing a book that I finished that big a chunk of. However, this one improved enough at about th</span>
  <span id="freeText10411705230141911193" style="display:none"><b>2.5 Stars (that last half star is for the parts in between 60-90%)<br />Don't hate me!!!!!!!</b><br /><br />Miss for me, for the most part. I almost stopped reading this one, in fact. My rule of thumb for dnf is that I must wait until I hit the 65% mark. If I still can't stand it enough by then and I'm able to skip the last 35% of the book, then it <i>really</i> isn't holding my interest. And I still feel justified rating and reviewing a book that I finished that big a chunk of. However, this one improved enough at about the halfway point that I really did want to figure out what was going to happen.<br /><br />Okay, (deep breath). I know that this seems to be a fan favorite, but I'm quite baffled by all of the high ratings. The editing was atrocious. I don't normally care about punctuation, but countless misspelled words and misused phrases leads me to believe that almost no one edited it at all. At least get a beta reader group or <i>something</i>. People pay money for your book. Show them your best, for goodness sake. Here is an example of a "Whaaaaa...?" moment from me:<br /><br /><b>"...I'm choking because you're sitting there staring at me like the taste of your turkey wrap depends on your life."</b><br /><br />...the taste of your turkey wrap depends on your life? Huh? Shouldn't it be "like your life depends on the taste of your turkey wrap?" Anyways, moving on...<br /><br />I could overlook editing, and often do with the massive amounts of indie authors that I read. In this book, however, that minor grump in addition to the high school bitch that is Grace and her best friend Lea and their overly dramatized reactions, many drunken escapades, and the fact that the paranormal aspect of the story (the only aspect that was interesting) was only alluded to for nearly half of the book...well, it made for an eye rolling read for me. <br /><br />There are massive amounts of drama; i.e., <b>bursting</b> into laughter over a silly joke, <b>screaming</b> into faces over perceived insults and/or minor infractions of date etiquette...everything was just overdone. I felt like I was watching a soap opera. <br /><br />There seems to be a trend lately in this 'new adult' sub genre to see who can come up with the most self-absorbed heroine, give her a real man whore who suddenly turns into Romeo, and then make her overreact to <b>every single situation and conversation</b> that she's involved in. I just can't stomach it. I have to actually <i>like</i> the main characters...at the very least be able to empathize with them, and I couldn't do it with Grace.<br /><br />Why was the paranormal aspect such a secret? For me, I could have overlooked a lot of this book's faults had I actually been interested in the story line. But the first half was really stagnant. After I found out what was really going on, the plot really picked up and I found myself interested to the point that I stayed up late to finish. So the book for me <i>vastly</i> improves after about fifty percent. <br /><br />There is a huge, nasty cliffhanger at the end....another star taken off, in my already grumpy opinion. And while I really do want to find out how this story ends, I have a feeling that if I don't read the book NOW, it will sit and wait on my virtual shelf for months, bugging me until I cave one future day and finally read it. I don't actually think I want to at this point but we'll see. <br /><br />To my buddy readers, sorry I stayed silent. I just didn't want to bee the Eeyore to your happy bunch. I know tons of people really dug this one, it just wasn't for me!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="10411705230141911193" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer459481852933672767"><b>Spoiler Free Review -A MUST READ</b><br/>4.5 STARS out of 5 <br/>Genre: Paranormal Romance/Fantasy-Contemporary Romance<br/><br/><i>'He was perfection. I couldn’t even have matched an adjective to him if I’d tried, but perfect would be the closest fit, and it still wasn’t good enough to describe him.'</i> ~Grace<br/><br/>Grace has been gone six months and now after her brother Jacob's death it's time to return home to New York city and her best friend Lea. Besides Jacob, Lea is the only one that knows who Grace really is. A secret Grac</span>
  <span id="freeText459481852933672767" style="display:none"><b>Spoiler Free Review -A MUST READ</b><br />4.5 STARS out of 5 <br />Genre: Paranormal Romance/Fantasy-Contemporary Romance<br /><br /><i>'He was perfection. I couldn’t even have matched an adjective to him if I’d tried, but perfect would be the closest fit, and it still wasn’t good enough to describe him.'</i> ~Grace<br /><br />Grace has been gone six months and now after her brother Jacob's death it's time to return home to New York city and her best friend Lea. Besides Jacob, Lea is the only one that knows who Grace really is. A secret Grace has kept for centuries. After six months naturally some things have changed. Lea has a new boyfriend, Connor, and it seems like he may be<i> the one</i>. The same night she is back in the city Grace meets up with Lea at Boozers. A local bar where Connor's friends will perform in their band Mad World. When the band starts Grace's breath immediately catches at the sight and voice of lead singer Shane.<br /><br />And honestly who can blame her the guy oozes sex appeal. He is known to have a different chick on his arm every night. Shane is the king of one night stands with the word monogamy missing from his life entirely. So of course it is fitting that he is the one to make Grace feel like no other man on Earth ever has.<br /><br />For a very very long time Grace has been searching for her long lost love and she will stop at nothing to be with him again. No matter how tempting Shane Maxton is. And believe me, the man is<i> OH SO TEMPTING!</i><br /> None of that matters to Grace, after centuries of living she now feels empty on the inside. And only one man can feel that void.<br /><br />It is evident that Shane was drawn to Grace like a moth to a flame. Although readers do not get his pov it was clear to see that he was falling for her. Falling hard and falling fast. Unfortunately, she rejected him at every turn letting him know that friendship would be the extent of their relationship. <br /><br />The connection between these two was palpable. The chemistry literally jumped off the pages and gripped the front of my shirt.<br />I continuously wondered how long she could resist him. Then I figured why not take him for a test drive? But nope she stood her ground and Shane would beg her to give in.<b> F**king BEG HER! </b><br /><br /><b>AGAIN...</b><br /> <br /><i> “One kiss, Grace, just one simple kiss. Baby, please,”</i> he begged.<i> “Just one.” </i> ~Shane<br /><br /><b>AND AGAIN...</b><br /><br /><i>“Grace... One kiss, please. Let me taste you,”</i> ~Shane<br /><br /><b>AND AGAIN...</b><br /><br /><i>“Please, Grace, whatever it is you’re going after, please try to find it here in me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be.”</i> ~Shane<br /><br />**Sighs heavily**<br /><br />And then he would do something like quote Shakespeare or say the most sweetest things, like<br /><br /><i>“Did my heart love till now? Forswear it sight, for I ne'er saw true beauty ‘til this night,”</i> ~Shane, quoting Shakespeare<br /><br /><i>“I have never seen anyone more exquisite in my entire life, Grace.   You seem to have this knack of making me completely... breathless.”</i> ~Shane<br /><br />None of that matters to Grace though, after centuries she feels empty on the inside... In her soul, she felt painfully empty.<br /><br /><b> <i> I wanted to scream. FORGET Grace, Shane, you can have me MIND BODY and SOUL.</i></b><br /> <br />This book left me breathless when I finished it! It was ABSOLUTELY FABULOUS and I truly wanted to kick myself for not reading it sooner. Readers get great character dynamics, lot's of witty banter, and a slow building<b> INFERNO</b> with Grace and Shane. The story will pull at your heart the entire length of the book.<br /><br />On the real...I am still too excited, I probably should of waited to write this review but I could not contain myself. I'll stop now so that I can keep it spoiler free. <br /><br />My Ratings<br />Characters- Lovable<br />Writing Style- Good, very witty, intense and at times emotional<br />Storyline/Plot- Savory, and Compelling<br />Steam Factor- High/Very Steamy<br />Overall- I LOVED IT! A MUST READ!!<br /><b><br />Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6706851978505707426">5 stars because I AM IN LOVE WITH SHANE MAXTON. I can not believe how much I loved Fall From Grace. There was no stopping once I started. <br/><br/>The only thing that I can say without spoiling it is Shane and Grace are both so frustratingly stubborn but I was cheering for them. The banter between the two was perfect. They are perfect together but they are both too stubborn to see it. <br/><br/>Shane is a rockstar covered in tattoos and oozes sexiness. He gets around but when he meets Grace, he knows that she's th</span>
  <span id="freeText6706851978505707426" style="display:none">5 stars because I AM IN LOVE WITH SHANE MAXTON. I can not believe how much I loved Fall From Grace. There was no stopping once I started. <br /><br />The only thing that I can say without spoiling it is Shane and Grace are both so frustratingly stubborn but I was cheering for them. The banter between the two was perfect. They are perfect together but they are both too stubborn to see it. <br /><br />Shane is a rockstar covered in tattoos and oozes sexiness. He gets around but when he meets Grace, he knows that she's the one that he has been looking for. He is so thoughtful and cares so much for Grace. I just wanted wrap him up in a big hug. <br /><br />Grace is so stubborn. She wants Shane but is to stubborn to admit. A couple of times I wanted to head butt her because man she is hard headed. <br /><br />The friends on both sides were the best. They stuck together and they were all very supportive.<br /><br />There is a major cliffhanger so I am on to the next soon. Too many secrets coming out and I need answers.<br /><br />This is a paranormal romance. The author mentioned it in the blurb but I almost missed it myself!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6594708628124329739"><span>[image error]</span><a href='http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/images-5.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

</a><br/><br/>This one snuck up on me!!!! Great story!!!!!! AND with a TWIST of PNR!!!!!!! Oh... and did I mention, I'm in LOVE with Shane Maxton!!!!! <br/><br/><b>
  <i>"Did my heart love till now? Forswear it sight, for I ne'er saw true beauty 'til this night," he murmured." ..."Shakespeare," I whispered.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Grace is a beautiful girl who just lost the last of her family. The story opens with her brother dying from cancer, at a hospice he's been in for the last six months. He was all she had left, as her paren</span>
  <span id="freeText6594708628124329739" style="display:none"><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/images-5.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910246i/3187458.jpg" alt=" photo images-5.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This one snuck up on me!!!! Great story!!!!!! AND with a TWIST of PNR!!!!!!! Oh... and did I mention, I'm in LOVE with Shane Maxton!!!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>"Did my heart love till now? Forswear it sight, for I ne'er saw true beauty 'til this night," he murmured." ..."Shakespeare," I whispered.</i>
</b><br><br>Grace is a beautiful girl who just lost the last of her family. The story opens with her brother dying from cancer, at a hospice he's been in for the last six months. He was all she had left, as her parents died in a car accident when she was just a girl. A car accident that killed her too, or should have. But years later, she is still here, and now, her only brother is gone too. <br><br>Now Grace heads back to New York City, back to her best friend, her only friend, Lea, to try to put her life back together. However, when she returns, Lea now has a new boyfriend, and he's "The One," so Connor spends most of his time at their apartment, and let's just say that Connor has some interesting friends. One her first night back, Grace finds herself at Boozer's Bar around the corner from her flat, hanging out with Lea and Connor, where she is introduced to his best friends... and members of Mad World, the Band performing at the bar that night. Guys all seem quite taken with Grace...and she with them.. especially the incredibly sexy and infamous womanizer Shane Maxton, the group's singer and guitarist. <br><br>But Grace is in no mood to get involved. And she certainly doesn't want to be a notch on someone's bedpost at this point in her life... because she is saving herself, for someone she's been searching for for a really long time. Shane's piercing blue eyes and alluring smile definitely catch her eye, but she is quite sure he is NOT the one she is looking for, so she does all she can to avoid him. But the more she pushes him away, the more interested he becomes. She even goes as far as accepting a date with one of Connor's friends, Tucker, who is also relentless in his pursuit of her.<br><br>Tucker Bevli, what can I say about this guy. He is good looking, wealthy and successful, and none other than.... a jerk? In fact, he was such a jerk that it was almost hard to believe. And I was even more shocked that Lea and Connor not only let her go out with him, but that they actually encouraged it. Ok, well maybe they weren't aware of the level of jerk he actually was, but I don't see how they could have overlooked that part of his personality. I mean they were all friends since high school. AnyWHOOO, LOL, let's just say that Tucker wasn't that guy she'd been waiting for. <br><br>Shane, though, she couldn't seem to shake off. In fact, she found herself unwillingly drawn to him. Even in his man-whoreish ways she couldn't seem to stay away from him. But really... who would want to. As Lea once said, "have you seen him with his shirt off?" And I have to say, I love the way they came together. I love Grace's surprise audition, and her incredible talent that blew them all away. She was such a cool character... I wanted to BE her, even with her tragic background. She was just one cool chick. And I loved the way she kept surprising Shane with her utter coolness... her running, her playing, her knowledge,<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[her bike, and her viriginity! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Shane Maxton was such an amazing character!!! TOTALLY HOT!!!! Gorgeous, talented, and completely smitten with Grace. I loved all of his quotes... as much as her ability to place them!!! I loved all of his heart-stopping qualities, and his beautiful heart-felt words to her. <br><b>
  <i><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">["No. I want you to tell me why you have a pair of broken angel wings on your shoulder. I want you to tell my why you cut your wrists and I want to know why and how you play and sing the way you do, <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.. but most of all I want you to tell me what I need to do to be a good enough man for you."</i>
</b><br><br>Shane reminded me so much of Travis from Beautiful Disaster. However, I wasn't too thrilled with the presence of that "Bone Room"!! *cringe*<br><br>I loved all of the members of the band Alex, Ethan and Brayden. I also loved Lea and Connor's characters. I even loved the twist of the plot in the story that brought Gabriel and Shamsiel into the thick of it!!! I loved being in Grace's head, hearing her thoughts. I often felt like I was experiencing her feelings myself. But I have to say that the sexual tension nearly killed me several times throughout the story... I was completely exhausted from it by the end. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ And when she ran off with Blake at the end, after being with Shane in the car, and he told her he "LOVED" her...  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I thought my head would just explode!!! <br><br><b>
  <i>"Please, Grace, whatever it is you're going after, please try to find it here in me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be."</i>
</b><br><br>FULL BODY SWOOOOOOOOONNNNN!!!!!!!!<br><br>The ending was nail-biting and mind-blowing. I was totally un-prepared for that!!!!!! Which actually added a half a star for me at the end. I LOVED the book, and was anxious to read the sequel. I highly recommend this book... especially to those who like a little PNR mixed into the plot!!!<br><br><b>
  <i>"I wake up with you as the last thought in my dreams. I dream about your lips, the smell of your skin and hair, and the freaking fire that burns inside of me to be inside of you. I want to bury myself inside of you and never climb out, my sweet death, Grace, I'm fucking in love with you."</i>
</b><br><br>DEATH BY SWOOOOOOOOOONNNNNNN!!!!!!!!!!!!!!<br><br><b>4.5 STARS!!!!!!!!!!! Great STORY!!!!!! I'm in LOVE!!!!!!!<br><br><b>Grace Taylor....</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/megan-fox-armani.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910246i/3187459._SY540_.jpg" alt="Megan Fox photo megan-fox-armani.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>Shane Maxton...(add some tats)</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/NickAyler_16334.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380910246i/3187460._SY540_.jpg" alt="Nick Ayler photo rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177925.jpg" alt=" photo FRAN6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><b>Lea Rossi...</b><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/AmberHeard997.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380909142i/3177926._SY540_.jpg" alt="Amber Heard photo AmberHeard997.jpg"   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/435965382" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/435965382?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer435965382" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15224721282630892504"><b>5 Stars!</b> Couldn’t put this one down! SO glad I can start this second one... it left me wanting more!!!<br/><br/><i>”She is a mortal danger to all men. She is beautiful without knowing it, and possesses charms that she’s not even aware of. She is like a trap set by nature- a sweet perfumed rose in whose petals Cupid lurks in ambush! Anyone who has seen her smile has known perfection. She instills grace in every common thing and divinity in every careless gesture. Venus in her shell was never so lovely, and Di</i></span>
  <span id="freeText15224721282630892504" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars!</b> Couldn’t put this one down! SO glad I can start this second one... it left me wanting more!!!<br /><br /><i>”She is a mortal danger to all men. She is beautiful without knowing it, and possesses charms that she’s not even aware of. She is like a trap set by nature- a sweet perfumed rose in whose petals Cupid lurks in ambush! Anyone who has seen her smile has known perfection. She instills grace in every common thing and divinity in every careless gesture. Venus in her shell was never so lovely, and Diana in the forest never so graceful as you.” </i><br /><br />This was an awesome love story with a small PNR twist, which I loved! <br />Grace just lost the last member of her family (except for her best friend Lea). She moves back to NYC after being with her brother at a hospice facility for 6 months. Lea is now dating Conner, who happens to have a fun group of friends who are constantly around. All the guys like Grace right away- especially Tucker (douche-bag ugh!) and the lead singer/swoon worthy Shane. Grace is at a point in ‘her life’ that she doesn’t want to get involved with anyone... especially someone like Shane who she thinks only wants one night with her. Grace has a past and secret that no one knows except Lea... when things/people from her past start to surface, she has some choices to make. <br /><b>
  <i> "No. I want you to tell me why you have a pair of broken angel wings on your shoulder. I want you to tell me why you cut your wrists. and I want to know wny and how you play and sing the way you do, but most of all I want you to tell me what i need to do to be a good enough man for you.” </i>
</b><br /><br />I’ll start with Shane... <b>Shane</b> I could not get enough of Shane! He was like a super combination of Travis Maddox(The Bone Room? Really lol) and Kellan Kyle(Lead singer of a band and super hot... check) Which equals the perfect swoon worthy bad, but not so bad boy! My new book boy for sure. He was so sweet with Grace, charming, funny and talented. And the Jeep part... holy hell! That was hot! He also had beautiful words in the book...<br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Please, Grace, whatever it is you’re going after, please try to find it in here in me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i> ”Stop smiling, Grace. A smile like that can give a man hope.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i> ” I wake up with you as the last thought in my dreams. I dream about your lips, the smell of your skin and hair, and the freaking fire that burns inside of me to be inside to be inside you. I want to bury myself inside you and never climb out, my sweet death. Grace, I’m fucking in love with you.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I also really liked Grace. She had a lot going on, and at times I wanted to scream at her, but overall I liked how she wasn’t afraid to speak her mind. She and Lea were so funny, loved the one liners in this one! <br /><br /><b>
  <i> He didn’t even come in to get me. Didn’t even call, just texted. Prince Freaking Uncharming. Strike one.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>He fist pumped. YES! I just said he fist pumped! I needed to get the hell away from this spiked hair, sushi eating, fist pumping jackass as soon as it was humanly possible.</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>”You know, if you’re going to be a smart ass you should start with being smart, otherwise, you’re really just an ass.”</i>
</b> <br /><br /><b>
  <i> “Don’t even try, because you might find me smacking the slut out of you in a minute!” </i>
</b><br /><br />The last 10%... <b>WOW</b> I about had a mini panic attack! I kinda had a feeling about how some of it went down, but some of it I was just like AHHH- Cliffhanger! I am going to get started on the second book asap! </span>
  <a data-text-id="15224721282630892504" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_433558673" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/433558673" />
    <a title="Erin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4979538-erin"><img alt="Erin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1520654483p2/4979538.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/433558673?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Erin" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Erin" href="/user/show/4979538-erin">Erin</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=romance-erotica-faves">romance-erotica-faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=favorite-authors">favorite-authors</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4979538-erin?shelf=books-that-changed-your-life-and-ma">books-that-changed-your-life-and-ma</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer433558673" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1169000378667795770">HOLY SWEET MOTHER OF ALL DELECTABLE SEXUAL TENSION WITH A HEAPING SIDE OF INCREDIBLE, HEART-STOPPING ROMANTIC TORTURE!!! My heart is beating out of my chest right now from the cliffhanger to shame all cliffhangers, but I must somehow get this review done before I get myself so far into the sequel Saving Grace that they start to mesh together! Five stars??!! Not nearly enough!!<br/><br/>First off, a standing ovation, high five, hand over the award now "Woot, woot!!" to Christine Zolendz for this absolutely</span>
  <span id="freeText1169000378667795770" style="display:none">HOLY SWEET MOTHER OF ALL DELECTABLE SEXUAL TENSION WITH A HEAPING SIDE OF INCREDIBLE, HEART-STOPPING ROMANTIC TORTURE!!! My heart is beating out of my chest right now from the cliffhanger to shame all cliffhangers, but I must somehow get this review done before I get myself so far into the sequel Saving Grace that they start to mesh together! Five stars??!! Not nearly enough!!<br /><br />First off, a standing ovation, high five, hand over the award now "Woot, woot!!" to Christine Zolendz for this absolutely incredible story! And what makes is so incredible, do you ask? The flawless recipe for an out-of-this world paranormal romance that leaves you breathless, that's what! Take bookgasm-worthy characters, an addicting plot that leaves you guessing, chemistry so intense that every minute is like the most maddening foreplay, and a torturous heart-thrashing that literally steals the air from your lungs, and you have this irresistible story! It's going to be difficult to talk about it in any detail without giving away what's behind the plot, but I don't want to ruin that surprise for anyone. Zolendz truly came up with a brilliant concept here, and I absolutely LOVED it!!!! <br /><br />Grace is one of those characters that just keeps you in a constant state of either awe, frustration, or sheer pride for her awesomeness. I went through so many emotions for and with her, and when the book came to a close I felt like I knew every corner of her mind. She's strong and thick-skinned thanks to the pain and heartache she's had to endure, she's the sassy and quick-witted best friend you've always wished you had, and underneath it all she's got this vixen that is dying to come out and play. I went into this one blind, not knowing what her "secret" was, and I LOVED the twist, so I'm not going to give it away. But it was totally unexpected as this story starts out like your typical tension-filled contemp romance, and my heart just melted for Grace. As much as I wanted to throttle her for her stubbornness and often aloof treatment of Shane, deep down I couldn't be angry with the woman given what she's had to endure. And through it all, the girl was just plain bad-ass and had the hilarious banter making me love her even more.<br /><br /><b> “Please, save your breath, because you might need it to blow up your date later.” ~Grace </b><br /><br />And Shane...there just aren't words adequate to describe this walking temptation!!! He's unbelievably sexy and sweet in his bad-boy way, and he stops at nothing to get Grace to feel something for him. The chemistry with these characters was blazing inferno hot just from the smoldering looks and sexy yet innocent touches they gave each other, and I couldn't believe how much my heart raced in this story from even the briefest of moments between them! I love my smut and I love steamy scenes like nobody's business, and I stand by the statement that Zolendz will do to your body with foreplay what EL James, Sylvia Day, and Gena Showalter do with full-blown explosive sex scenes!! It was incredibly addicting!!<br /><br /><b> “No. I want you to tell me why you have a pair of broken angel wings on your shoulder. I want you to tell me why you cut your wrists and I want to know why and how you play and sing the way you do, but most of all I want you to tell me what I need to do to be a good enough man for you.”~Shane </b><br /><br />The whole bar and apartment setting made for one party session after another for these characters, and I loved the boys in Shane's band Mad World. They were sweet but all had a certain edge that made them so swoon-worthy!! And Grace's best friend Lea was another awesome character, always being the support and partner in crime when she needed it. After all the loss Grace had experienced, having Lea was the one constant that grounded her and gave her something to be happy about in a truly messed-up world. <br /><br />I was literally glued to my iPad for the day as I read this story, because it was almost physically painful to leave it behind!! Steaminess and sexual tension aside, the mystery behind the twists and the heartbreaking torment for both Grace and Shane had my stomach just in knots. Imagine that torturous forbidden love, jealousy, and drama that you find in your favorite love stories, and ratchet that up several notches and spread that across an entire story...yes, this one is very hard on the pulse!! It was blissfully perfect torment, and I relished in every moment of their self-inflicted pain because it was obvious how much they were meant to be together. That fact alone made the suffering that much more intense, and I just ate it up!! Perfection!!<br /><br />I'm going to stop this now, because I flew right into Saving Grace after reading this and now I'm simply crazed needing to go back to it!! This series is an ABSOLUTE MUST-READ, and it's shot it's way into my top 5 favorite PNR for sure...scratch that, even higher!! Awesome, incredible, unforgettable, astounding...READ IT NOW!!!! </span>
  <a data-text-id="1169000378667795770" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Kristy Mills" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2079018-kristy-mills"><img alt="Kristy Mills" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1253471111p2/2079018.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/440450821?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kristy Mills" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kristy Mills" href="/user/show/2079018-kristy-mills">Kristy Mills</a>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer3807241039951560074">Wow this was soOOO GOOD!!! So I bought this book and thought I would just read the first chapter or two before going to bed. This was around midnight. The next thing I know, my room is getting brighter and the birds are chirping and it's time to wake the kids up for school!<br/><br/><a href='http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&current=tumblr_m9gwpbTS2L1rc4xhwo1_500.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText3807241039951560074" style="display:none">Wow this was soOOO GOOD!!! So I bought this book and thought I would just read the first chapter or two before going to bed. This was around midnight. The next thing I know, my room is getting brighter and the birds are chirping and it's time to wake the kids up for school!<br><br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m9gwpbTS2L1rc4xhwo1_500.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395288ra/761289.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Great, now I have a day of THIS to look forward to...<br><br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=when-you-wake-up-the-next-day-after-partying-all-night.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395288ra/761290.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>BUT FIRST, I had to finish the book. So I got the kids up, got them on the bus and read the last few pages... can you believe that?! I only had a couple pages left. I didn't know this when I got out of bed, but I'll get to that later. I'm getting ahead of myself.<br><br>This book was about a girl named Grace. Grace has been jumping from life to life, body to body for centuries in search of a man. She is searching for her other half, her soul mate. The man whose kiss gave her a glimpse of heaven. That kiss is also the reason they were punished and destined to live for centuries searching for each other.<br><br>Grace has just lost the last family member she has, in the life she is living in at the moment. Her brother has just died of cancer and the only person she has left in the world is her best friend Lea. After 6 months of taking care of her brother she moves back to NYC with Lea. Since Grace has been gone Lea has fallen in love and has a a whole new circle of friends to introduce Grace to. This circle of friends is an up and coming rock band and when Grace first hears lead singer Shane sing she is immediately captivated. As she gets to know Shane, he stirs feelings in her that she hasn't felt in centuries. Shane is a womanizer and jumps from bed to bed. And no matter how much her body thinks it wants Shane, she will not allow herself to be used. She refuses to waste her time on a commitment phobe when she knows there is a man out there who loves her and longs for her as much as she does him. But Shane doesn't seem to want to take no for an answer. Not only is he a relentless flirt, but he starts showing signs of jealousy and is very protective of Grace, shocking all of their friends.<br><br>This book was HOTT!!! With steamy scenes, but surprisingly never went very far. No sex scenes. But emotionally high make out scenes. <br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_liouv5WgHN1qbni9q.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395288ra/761291.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Then there was the whole music aspect of the book, that I LOVE. There was lots of angst and overall a cool concept for a story. So obviously I couldn't put the book down. It moved along at a pretty fast pace, my eyes were glued to my Kindle screen until my alarm clock rang. Fast forward... I get my kids on the bus, slam the front door, run and cannonball on the couch and get back to the book. (I didn't even stop in the kitchen for coffee.) I left off at a pretty major part of the story and then JUST when it was getting good, everything that had been building throughout the book was FINALLY being revealed and I excitedly turned the page and read . . .<br><br><i>Come visit me on my blog . . . </i><br><br><br><br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lm7mnuDbGb1qbigyv.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395288ra/761292.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_m8593oypzW1rc4xhwo1_250.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380395288ra/761293.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

</a><br><br>When the shock started to wear off and the red haze that had clouded my vision began to clear and I continued to read down a few lines where she said . . . <br><br><i>I promise you that there will be a book 2!</i> <br><br>I frantically grabbed my Macbook and jumped on amazon and book 2 is already WRITTEN! <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070072.Saving_Grace__Mad_World___2_" title="Saving Grace (Mad World, #2) by Christine Zolendz" rel="nofollow noopener">Saving Grace </a><br><br><a href="http://s7.photobucket.com/albums/y277/peedletuck/Blog%20and%20goodreads/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lnktwcb5KE1qf092no1_250.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

I can't even think about closing my eyes now.<br><br>This book just captivated me, it was definitely my kind of book. Sorry this is not a very well thought out review and it feels rushed, but I can't stop thinking about the book that is sitting on my Kindle waiting for me to read. I HAVE to find out what happens to Shane and Grace.   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/432624383?book_show_action=true">Oct 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Georgia ♥ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Georgia ♥ " href="/user/show/9138738-georgia">Georgia ♥ </a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9138738-georgia?shelf=another-freaking-cliffhanger">another-freaking-cliffhanger</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer432624383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3878799544888802207"><b>4+ Angels Among Us Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393705i/758062._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='357' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>In the beginning of time, before the world becomes old, God was merciful and vengeful, at the same time and angels were still pure. A small band of them was stationed on Earth to help the humans, but they were corrupted. They fell in love with the women and they gave birth to abominations. The giants, the Nephelim. There were no other choice. God punished them. They fell from grace and they were imprisoned in hell. And their human women were punished along them. But, ther</span>
  <span id="freeText3878799544888802207" style="display:none"><b>4+ Angels Among Us Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380393705i/758062._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="357" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>In the beginning of time, before the world becomes old, God was merciful and vengeful, at the same time and angels were still pure. A small band of them was stationed on Earth to help the humans, but they were corrupted. They fell in love with the women and they gave birth to abominations. The giants, the Nephelim. There were no other choice. God punished them. They fell from grace and they were imprisoned in hell. And their human women were punished along them. But, there was a couple that was pure. Shamsiel and Selah. Their only crime? A single kiss, that doomed them for all eternity. Selah never got to die. She became a lost soul, cursed to live in the empty shells that people left behind, forced to look for a pair of warm blue eyes throughout eternity.<br><br><i>
  <b>“There’s no book; fictional, horror, fairytale, anything that could come even close to the warped disturbing reality of my horrible existence.”</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394070ra/758712.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, she is <b>Grace</b> and she is weary. She longs for the peace and tranquility that is heaven. She has given up hope, but she can’t help still looking and fooling herself that she will find him again. When she loses her human brother, ready to move forward once again, another pair or blues eyes, this time icy and cold will awaken her slumbering heart and make her stubborn head wonder if she should give up after all and betray the memory of her angel. But she has to make the most out of the Grace’s life and hope that someone up there will take pity on her suffering, never realizing that she is brighter than any star she wishes to.<br><br><i>
  <b>“Grace, you have never and will never quietly exist. You shine on earth as if the sun was born here. You have been a beacon for all of humanities sufferings and exhilarations.”</b>
</i><br><br>But she can’t trust and she has suffered so much to take a huge leap of faith. So she may end up into the hands of a madman…<br><br><b>Shane Maxton</b>, rockstar and manwhore extraordinaire, is the reason that Grace is now questioning her deep-rooted beliefs and she is ready to give up her search. But Shane isn’t an easy man to love. An arrogant, tattooed and talented bad boy, cynical as he is caring and daring and protective, he will lay his own heart at Grace’s feet hoping for a miracle that wasn’t granted to him long ago, when he too lost his own love.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394070ra/758713.gif" width="400" height="320" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two proud people, a passion that can’t be denied, a murderous plot made in heaven and so much heartbreak, make for an exciting read. Haunting and eerie, beautiful, tender and romantic, totally badass and hip, this book grabbed me from the first page, until the heartbreaking finale. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394070ra/758714.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>♪♫I stand there <br>And no one knew me<br>I reach for her <br>She looks right through me<br>I can search this world over <br>She can’t see me I drown in tears <br>They look right through me♪♫</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Grace’s stubbornness and refusal to love and be loved, frustrated and hooked me at the same time and Shane was just too delicious to resist. The sexual tension was smoldering and you could feel their scorching chemistry through the pages. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380394070ra/758715.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Definitely a book that deserves your attention! Thank God the next is out!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380393858ra/758350.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></span>

<div id="review_648223336" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/648223336" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/648223336?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=june-reads">june-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer648223336" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10267500840370309012">This book was a pleasant surprise for me..First of all, I obviously do not pay much attention..I thought this was a Contemporary Romance, and instead, slowly I started to figure out there was some kind of paranormal aspects to this story. The full story of who Grace is takes its time being revealed, so I was constantly trying to figure things out in my brain!! This added a pleasant mystery for me, as well as keeping me on my toes! The whole book kept me entertained, and it had a bunch of factors</span>
  <span id="freeText10267500840370309012" style="display:none">This book was a pleasant surprise for me..First of all, I obviously do not pay much attention..I thought this was a Contemporary Romance, and instead, slowly I started to figure out there was some kind of paranormal aspects to this story. The full story of who Grace is takes its time being revealed, so I was constantly trying to figure things out in my brain!! This added a pleasant mystery for me, as well as keeping me on my toes! The whole book kept me entertained, and it had a bunch of factors that are popular in a lot of the romance books we love today.<br />First of all, we have Grace who suffers from a lot of loss in her life. She is actually in search of her long lost love whom she is hoping that one day will come into her life again. Her best friend and roomate is dating a guy who is very good buds with a fellow named Shane Maxton. Now Shane is in a band called, "Mad World," he is beyond HOT, has sexy tattoes, and knows his way around women..(I would say probably WAY too much!!) He even has a room in his apartment called, "The Bone Room," I am sure you can figure out exactly what that room is used for!! He is so use to the ladies falling at his feet, but when Grace gives him the cold shoulder it turns into his mission to find out how to be the man she wants him to be.<br />Even though Grace has a chip on her shoulder when it comes to Shane, she is extremely attracted to him. When they are together, they seem to be the only ones in the room, and sparks fly. She puts up a great fight against her "lust" though, I am not sure that I would have that kind of restraint! When one of the band members becomes hurt, Grace surprises the band at the auditions and she becomes the temporary guitar player. As this all plays out, things are not all what they seem, and there are many reveals that take place throughout the story. There is never a dull moment, and I loved every minute of it!<br />This book offers everything from friendship, romance, humor, and at times tears. The date that Grace goes on with one of the guys in their circle of friends was hilarious. I was laughing so hard when I was picturing Grace's speaker phone turning on as her friends are yelling at her..Tucker (her date) did not take it well at all, but every single person in that restaurant was highly interested in all that was going on! Just priceless!! My only complaint, which really doesn't end up to be an issue considering Book two is already out..There is a cliffie at the end..I could definitely say that if the second book wasn't out yet, I probably would have been very upset! Needless to say, I have started Number two immediately, and can't wait to see what Grace, Shane, and their friends are up to this time! This is a highly entertaining series that I will for sure be adding to my keeper shelf. There is some very steamy parts in the book as well; but it is more "PG" rated than "R"!! Who knows what the next book will bring to the table as far as sex..I am hoping for a little more sparks; but I shall see what Christine Zolendz has in store for us in the next installment; but I am sure whatever it is it will have me hooked from start to finish! I can't wait!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10267500840370309012" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>
