<div id="review_382879993" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/382879993" />
    <a title="Sam" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2894540-sam"><img alt="Sam" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1319826913p2/2894540.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/382879993?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sam" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sam" href="/user/show/2894540-sam">Sam</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer382879993" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15197482292410945213">I can’t even say how much I loved this book. It was like Beautiful Disaster meets Thoughtless meets Supernatural. Can you get any better than that? Okay, so Travis, Kellan, Sam and Dean aren’t featured in the book (how cool would THAT be???) but you get my point. I started reading it when I got home from work and the rest of the evening went like this:<br/><br/>Heathen Childeren: “Mom”<br/>Me: “Reading”<br/>HC: “What’s for dinner”<br/>M: “Reading”<br/>HC: “Mom, seriously I am starved, what is for dinner”<br/>M: “Seriously, are yo</span>
  <span id="freeText15197482292410945213" style="display:none">I can’t even say how much I loved this book. It was like Beautiful Disaster meets Thoughtless meets Supernatural. Can you get any better than that? Okay, so Travis, Kellan, Sam and Dean aren’t featured in the book (how cool would THAT be???) but you get my point. I started reading it when I got home from work and the rest of the evening went like this:<br /><br />Heathen Childeren: “Mom”<br />Me: “Reading”<br />HC: “What’s for dinner”<br />M: “Reading”<br />HC: “Mom, seriously I am starved, what is for dinner”<br />M: “Seriously, are your arms broken, make a sandwich”<br />HC: “Mom”<br />M: “No talking allowed”<br /><br />Yeah, so I didn't get the Betty Crocker and Mother of the Evening award that night, but I read a really great book.<br /><br />Grace is tough and she doesn’t take shit off of anyone and I love that about her. Grace isn’t looking for a relationship; well she is, just with ONE person in particular. She has got a mental picture of her mystery guy, who happens to have a certain facial feature. She refuses to get involved with anyone who isn’t her…well you have to figure that out.<br />Shane, sigh, Shane is our smokin’ hot, bad boy. He sings in a band so he has his flavor of the day. This is evidenced by the room in his house named “The Bone Room”. Shane is pretty dreamy. Who doesn’t love a gorgeous guy who sings in a band? He is also tender and sweet with Grace but doesn’t hesitate to go all badass on anyone who is trying to hurt her.<br />The chemistry between these two is explosive and you could cut the sexual tension with a knife. I found myself getting emotionally involved with the two of them, rooting for them, and hollering at the stubbornness of some of their actions. <br />"I heard the floor boards creak on the other side of my door. I could hear his breath, "Grace..."Then something hard thumped against the door right above my head. I pictured Shane in the same position as me with our faces almost touching but for the inch of wood between us"<br />I really can’t say too much more without giving the book away which would be a cryin’ shame, so go buy it. It is a what a bargain at $1.50. Fair warning it does have a cliffhanger ending, but the author is furiously writing another book. I think I might send my kids to babysit hers, so she can write faster.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="15197482292410945213" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15542671374960117210">5 'I am in love with this story' stars.<br/><br/>I don't know how I will write a review with the ending I've just experienced my poor, poor book heart. Angels, immortality, love, heart ache, I've not got words to give this book justice ... But here are some Lisa thoughts.<br/><br/>I've not really had a huge experience of reading paranormal romance, but after having a recommendation i'm glad I gave this book my attention, I 100% enjoyed and fell in LOVE with this GORGEOUS story.<br/><br/>It was a real mixed bag of emotions an</span>
  <span id="freeText15542671374960117210" style="display:none">5 'I am in love with this story' stars.<br /><br />I don't know how I will write a review with the ending I've just experienced my poor, poor book heart. Angels, immortality, love, heart ache, I've not got words to give this book justice ... But here are some Lisa thoughts.<br /><br />I've not really had a huge experience of reading paranormal romance, but after having a recommendation i'm glad I gave this book my attention, I 100% enjoyed and fell in LOVE with this GORGEOUS story.<br /><br />It was a real mixed bag of emotions and themes. It was funny but heart wrenching, sexy but touching, real but supernatural, emotional but easy reading, bitter sweet but addictive, all in one amazing well written package.<br /><br />This is a moving, story of TRUE soul mates and the journey of finding their way back to each other. My heart was swept up completely in this story.I don't think I've enjoyed characters so much in one book as this author gave us, it's intriguing and intense and there's more sexual tension than my heart could manage, but I can assure you that i am head over with this book. If you like your book boyfriends then look no further - Shane Maxton is off the scales lovely and with an equally amazing female lead I was in book heaven (pun intended)! ... Off to read book #2 <br /><br />5 HUGE stars and a new found love for PNR.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer393756127" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7075618102796950125"><b>OH MY GOD, THIS BOOK IS AMAZING!!!!!</b><br/><br/>It’s 2.45am and I’ve just finished this book after reading it in one sitting. I absolutely could not put it down. Fantastic banter, sarcastic humour and EPIC angst and sexual tension, there's also a strong supernatural element to things just to make things extra interesting. I was glued from start to finish, and my heart pounded pretty much all the way through. I’m so freaking excited that I can’t even write a proper review, just a quick gush.<br/><br/>Grace is not your</span>
  <span id="freeText7075618102796950125" style="display:none"><b>OH MY GOD, THIS BOOK IS AMAZING!!!!!</b><br /><br />It’s 2.45am and I’ve just finished this book after reading it in one sitting. I absolutely could not put it down. Fantastic banter, sarcastic humour and EPIC angst and sexual tension, there's also a strong supernatural element to things just to make things extra interesting. I was glued from start to finish, and my heart pounded pretty much all the way through. I’m so freaking excited that I can’t even write a proper review, just a quick gush.<br /><br />Grace is not your ordinary girl. She has a secret, a big one, and it's one that has kept her closed off for most of her life. When her best friend drags her out to meet her new boyfriend, she also meets his friend, Shane, and the two of them are drawn to each other in a way that surprises them both. But Shane is a commitment-phobic manwhore, and Grace once experienced a soul-changing, forever kind of love and still suffers from it's loss, and she refuses open her heart to anybody until she finds it again. <br /><br />The stage is set for an epic battle as Grace and Shane fall and fall hard for each other, with Grace trying hard to protect her heart, and Shane trying to convince her that she can trust him.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> “Please Grace, whatever it is you're going after, please try to find it here in me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Swoooooon!<br /><br />OMG, these characters are sensational! Shane is utter tattooed, rock-god, man whore perfection! Like a combination of Travis Maddox and Kellan Kyle. God, no wonder I fell in instant love with him! Grace is a very complex character, but I absolutely loved her, and the chemistry between her and Shane is freakishly intense. My heart was pounding through a number of their little ‘moments’, and I kept screeching at my kindle for them to JUST GET IT ON ALREADY!!!!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i> “Tell me. Tell me, Grace, that you don't feel this. Please. Tell me and I will walk right out of here”</i>
</blockquote><br />By the time they actually kissed I had worked myself up into a ridiculous frenzy that I squeed and cheered for them! But the pacing of it all was brilliant, and I loved the way it played out. And the banter! Oh so much banter, awesome!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Hey, you coming to the bar tonight?” he called out after me.<br /> I stopped and turned around, “Maybe, I don’t know. I have to see how I feel after a shower.”<br /> A smile burst onto his face, making him more stunning than it was humanly possible. “Do you need help with that? I’d like to see how you feel after a shower too…” </i>
</blockquote><br />The boys from the band were sensational, as was Grace's best friend, Lea. All of them hilarious, and gorgeously caring and supportive.<br /><br />The whole paranormal aspect is hinted at as you go along, and you pick up little clues here and there until the big reveal. It’s a fantastic concept, I really loved it.<br /><br />I laughed, I swooned and I squeed, and then that gut-wrenching ending! OMG, talk about your cliffhangers. Thank God I’ve got the next book on standby and can start it straight away. MUST.HAVE.MORE!!!<br /><br />5 sensational stars!<br /><br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer8375562916204395268"><b>DNF</b><br/>Here is the thing. I hardly ever DNF and can probably count on one hand the times I have given up on a book and I feel a little presumptuous rating it considering I read a little less than 50% of it. So please let me explain myself.<br/><br/><b>HONESTLY I JUST COULD'NT DO IT ANY MORE!</b><br/><a href='http://s1316.photobucket.com/user/2beechwood/media/shootmyself_zps0a5d24b0.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>

  <span id="freeText8375562916204395268" style="display:none"><b>DNF</b><br>Here is the thing. I hardly ever DNF and can probably count on one hand the times I have given up on a book and I feel a little presumptuous rating it considering I read a little less than 50% of it. So please let me explain myself.<br><br><b>HONESTLY I JUST COULD'NT DO IT ANY MORE!</b><br><a href="http://s1316.photobucket.com/user/2beechwood/media/shootmyself_zps0a5d24b0.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I have read a lot of books with editing and grammar issue and have always overlooked them. But this book takes it to a whole other level! It also doesn't help that I found everything (and I actually mean this literally) about this book either brain meltingly boring or nails on the chalk board irritating. Every detail was played out in "soap opera" style drama but lacked the foundation of real emotions or the back up of proper characterizations.<br><br>But ultimately what made me stop reading was when I realized that this book had a cast of genuinely unlikable characters. And I thought to myself- <b>What could possibly happen in the second half of this book that could make me like <u>any</u> of them or care what happens to them? And when the answer was a resounding <i>Nothing!</i> I knew I had to stop reading.</b></span>

    <a title="Kellie Maddox-Ward" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7309666-kellie-maddox-ward"><img alt="Kellie Maddox-Ward" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366371073p2/7309666.jpg" /></a>

He was still shirtless and the blonde had the biggest set of silicone breasts I had ever seen in real life. They are the equivalent of a blow up doll with brains to match." <br><br>"What the hell does that mean?" Blondie snapped. <br><br>"See you just proved my point." Lea looked at me and smiled. "Maybe if we use big words, it will leave?" <br><br>I shrugged and laughed. "Lea, you know you should never have a battle of wits with an unarmed opponent."<br><br>"Shut up, skanks! You're both just jealous." Blondie yelped, puffing her giant silicone chest out at us. <br><br>"Slut," Lea smiled. <br><br>I gave the blonde a serious face. "Yeah, listen you should really stop now, because I'm betting on the smartest thing that ever could come out of your mouth is penis." <br><br>Lea lost it and the water she was drinking burst from her mouth and landed all over blonde Amazon breast girl. <br><br> </blockquote> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453700564ra/17860130.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>She goes on to be extremely rude and judgement toward Shane, too. <br><br>The next night they all go out again and the Mc and Lea are right back to picking fights and bullying all the other girls around them... Again. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1453700564ra/17860131.gif" width="250" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I'm not into bitchy, mean girl, holier than though MCs who gang up on, insult, bully, and slut shame EVERY other female, especially when no one has done anything to them At All! That's what the OW are supposed to be like, not the MC. <br><br>10% in and yet another drunken bar scene. This time some dude pokes a knife in her back and tries to sexually assault her. <span id="freeTextContainer15779197779078348674">This review has me stumped! Yes, the girl who can't stop words (usually inappropriate) from flying out of her mouth has been stumped! Shee-it! I'm even referring to myself in third person. I may have even read some other people's reviews thinking maybe they would tell me how I should feel! So how do I feel??<br/><br/>It was good damn it!!!   <span id="freeText15779197779078348674" style="display:none">This review has me stumped! Yes, the girl who can't stop words (usually inappropriate) from flying out of her mouth has been stumped! Shee-it! I'm even referring to myself in third person. I may have even read some other people's reviews thinking maybe they would tell me how I should feel! So how do I feel??<br /><br />It was good damn it!!! Let's just get that out of the way right now! I picked it up and didn't put it down until I was finished. So why am I humping the leg of indifference??? The pacing was a little off; things kind of jumbled together and the paranormal element didn't flow and blend with the "real life" aspect of the storyline. Also, the editing comb could have been ran through a few tangles. However, I didn't let that affect my rating; just an observation. I could tell by the execution, that this was a new author, but I can see great things to come.<br /><br />I feel like the reason I can't make a decision is because I can see so much f**king potential with this book. Am I rating the actual book or the potential I see in it?? My mind is f**king with itself! <br /><br />Here's what I <i>can</i> tell you. I liked it, I'm glad I read it (for $1.50 it was a steal), I will be reading this author again, and that damn cliffhanger ENSURES I will be grabbing the sequel!! <br /><br />If you're hungry for a unique paranormal romance, with sexual tension, and a hot bad boy musician then <i>Fall from Grace</i> will fill you up! Mmmmmmm!<br /><br />READ ON!</span>

Maybe that's not the perfect word I'l use to describe it. Rather this was such a fucking hot book. Like the sexual tension in this book was so high I just wanted them to just get into bed and get it over w</span>
  <span id="freeText9593931505088776471" style="display:none">I am so freaking excited to start this book!!!!!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445013614ra/16587149.gif" width="500" height="300" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>*Edit* </i><br><br><b>Actual Ratings=5+++++++ rocking stars!!!</b><br><br>Oh my god. Like seriously, what did I just read?????I haven't liked a book like this in a looooooong time. This book was just, awesome. No other words to explain it.<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605546.gif" height="350" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was such a beautiful book. Maybe that's not the perfect word I'l use to describe it. Rather this was such a fucking hot book. Like the sexual tension in this book was so high I just wanted them to just get into bed and get it over with. I'm sure even then it wouldn't be over. All of it and they only freaking kissed!!!!! This has to be the first book I've ever read that has so much sexual tension between two people without having them do anything. <br><br>Now let me begin my review. This book is basically about <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ a human being punished to walk earth fro falling in love with an angel. So far she has been walking for 2000 years with no luck at all.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> First of all I would say that it's really sad how Grace was just sooooo cool. I loved how she kept rebuffing Shane (unfortunately for us). She was such an awesome character to read. If I had a off like her I would totally love. She was so cool and I love the fact that she sympathised for the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[real Grace <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> She was such an awesome girl who knew just how well she should play her cards. The only problem was how she didn't get the guy and see what was right infront of her eyes the whole time. I mean we all saw that one coming from the beginning of the book. <br>Then we have our beautiful Shane. Damn boy, you should have at least not taken all those girls home infront of Grace <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ even though you didn't do anything, technically  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> He was the most scarred <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Fallen angel  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> out there. I mean his life was in a mess and he had his heart ripped out. It was so obvious he was still hurting from how they were thrown apart ages ago. It was really sad how he didn't know that she was punished as well as him though. He sounded so heartbroken by then end of everything. My only problem, why was his eyes a different colour? Now here is an example of my version of Shane ;)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605547.gif" height="350" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>When it comes to tall brooding hot guys you just can't go wrong with Lachowski.<br><br> The other characters were awesome too. I really wished that we could have met Jacob cuz he sounds like an awesome brother And then Lea and Connor were such sweethearts. I didn't like the fact that everytime a band member walked her home, they tried to get a date out of her. Like guys trying to hump the prettiest girl you've met. I even liked Tucker. I liked how obnoxious he was. That made me dislike him faster but I would say the story would be missing a piece if he wasn't there. I really liked Ethan and I wish we get a book to see how he finds his happily ever after. He was a sweet pea (i can't believe I wrote that)<br><br>Now let me tell you the most interesting part of the book. THE FUCKING TENSION BETWEEN THEM&gt; SEXUAL TENSION!!! Now that was like O! M! G! I repeat, never have I read a book this hot and there was zero sex in it. The book had sex oozing out of it without having actual sex scenes in it. Damn Christine, you know how to write a book.<br><b>"She is a mortal danger to all men, She is beautiful without knowing it &amp; possesses charm that she's not even aware of. She is like a trap set by nature a sweet perfumed rose in whose petals Cupid lurks in ambush. Anyone who has seen her smile has known perfection, She instills grace in every common thing &amp; divinity in every careless gesture. Venus in her shell was never so lovely &amp; Diana in the forest never so graceful as you" </b><br>Shane you know how to romance a girl. Though in this case you failed in a small way.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605548.gif" height="350" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Every single time he totally opened up to Grace, I was brought to tears. He had been so devastated after Selah and it was so damn sad.<br><br><b>"Please, Grace, whatever it is you're going after, please try and find it here with me. I will try my best to be the man that you need me to be." </b><br> <br>How can you say no to him Grace, other than the fact he's a total manwhore. But god how i wanted them to be together.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605549.gif" height="350" width="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605550.gif" height="350 width=" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hot damn!!! <br>I've got so many gifs for this but let's not make this review inappropriate.<br>But that cliffhanger got me like<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1445137843ra/16605551.gif" width="450" height="350" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yeah Jimmy you got it right. And I have to wait for three weeks to get the second book. Maybe longer. I'm gonna die. Like literally :(<br>For you lucky people who have these two books within reach, GO NOW!!!! buy it, read it, live it, love it and then die within your happy bubble -.-</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/379536141?book_show_action=true">Jul 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=sup-suspense-romance">sup-suspense-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer379536141" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11270194970973025492">I loved this book. I could not put it down and I did not mind the ending as I am so excited to read the next book. The story had enough "rock star" bad boy feel, angsty misunderstanding, sexual tension, and paranormal mystery to hook me in and take me under for a page turning ride. Yes, I think it did have a bit of BD, Thoughtless and a little Providence vibe going, but for me it also had a little "The Opportunist" feeling as well. </span>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZQbsyXrMeMuMIilUnSTJ/O7Z6O233/0B5LgoFz7hheNqvjTfzpSV1f2Gxi5DjghMptLKUbjtFEGfLJ51m5syHw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ZdBB6+qC+Z/TTB9cmmEXLRjDKlR9KCXB7tvBNrC9tX5qaJn9XtoUgaLo8CZEy9adUMgI6HIazIGVT3dUFccCgg==')})
  }

You fall in love with him, of course.Pagan Moore doesn\'t cheat Death, but instead, falls in love with him.Seventeen year old Pagan Moore has seen souls her entire life. Once she realized the strangers she often saw walking through walls were not visible to anyone else, she started ignoring them. If she didn\'t let them know she could see them, then they left her alone. Until she stepped out of her car the first day of school and saw an incredibly sexy guy lounging on a picnic table, watching her with an amused smirk on his face. Problem is, she knows he\'s dead.Not only does he not go away when she ignores him, but he does something none of the others have ever done. He speaks. Pagan is fascinated by the soul. What she doesn\'t realize is that her appointed time to die is drawing near and the wickedly beautiful soul she is falling in love with is not a soul at all.He is Death and he\'s about to break all
